### Public servants, the military and the church {#Public_servants.2C_the_military_and_the_church}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=38 "Edit section: Public servants, the military and the church")\]

* [Conrad Justinger](/wiki/Conrad_Justinger "Conrad Justinger") ( 1360--1438) -- chronicler, magistrate and notary public of the city of Bern
* [Johann Jakob Grynaeus](/wiki/Johann_Jakob_Grynaeus "Johann Jakob Grynaeus") (1540--1617) -- Protestant divine, a theologian of the school of [Huldrych Zwingli](/wiki/Huldrych_Zwingli "Huldrych Zwingli")^[\[65\]](#cite_note-71)^{#cite_ref-71}
* [Robert Scipio, Freiherr von Lentulus](/wiki/Robert_Scipio_von_Lentulus "Robert Scipio von Lentulus") (1714--1786) -- military officer, in Austrian and later, Prussian service
* [Emmanuel Han](/wiki/Emmanuel_Han "Emmanuel Han") (1801--1867) -- military officer and [philhellene](/wiki/Philhellene "Philhellene"), fought in the [Greek War of Independence](/wiki/Greek_War_of_Independence "Greek War of Independence")
* [Walter Breisky](/wiki/Walter_Breisky "Walter Breisky") (1871--1944) -- Austrian jurist, civil servant and politician
* [Rosalie Dreyer](/wiki/Rosalie_Dreyer "Rosalie Dreyer") (1895--1987) -- naturalized British nurse, pioneer in Britain's public-funded nursing service
* [August R. Lindt](/wiki/August_R._Lindt "August R. Lindt") (1905--2000) -- lawyer and diplomat, Chairman of [UNICEF](/wiki/UNICEF "UNICEF") 1953--1954 and [UN High Commissioner for Refugees](/wiki/United_Nations_High_Commissioner_for_Refugees "United Nations High Commissioner for Refugees") 1956--1960
* [Marc Hodler](/wiki/Marc_Hodler "Marc Hodler") (1918--2006) -- lawyer, President of the International Ski Federation 1951--1998, exposed the [2002 Winter Olympic bid scandal](/wiki/2002_Winter_Olympic_bid_scandal "2002 Winter Olympic bid scandal")
* [Hans Urwyler](/wiki/Hans_Urwyler "Hans Urwyler") (1925--1994) -- Christian minister of the [New Apostolic Church](/wiki/New_Apostolic_Church "New Apostolic Church")
* [Kofi Annan](/wiki/Kofi_Annan "Kofi Annan") (1938--2018 in Bern) -- UN Secretary-General 1997--2006
* [Algirdas Paleckis](/wiki/Algirdas_Paleckis "Algirdas Paleckis") (born 1971) -- Lithuanian diplomat, politician and columnist

### Politicians and the landed gentry {#Politicians_and_the_landed_gentry}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=39 "Edit section: Politicians and the landed gentry")\]

* [Adrian von Bubenberg](/wiki/Adrian_von_Bubenberg "Adrian von Bubenberg") ( 1434--1479) -- Bernese knight, military commander and 3-time mayor (Schultheiss) of Bern, hero of the [Battle of Murten](/wiki/Battle_of_Murten "Battle of Murten")
* [Niklaus Dachselhofer](/wiki/Niklaus_Dachselhofer "Niklaus Dachselhofer") (1595--1670) -- Bernese politician, Schultheiss (mayor) of Bern 1636--1667
* [Christoph von Graffenried, 1st Baron of Bernberg](/wiki/Christoph_von_Graffenried,_1st_Baron_of_Bernberg "Christoph von Graffenried, 1st Baron of Bernberg") (1661--1743) -- founder of [New Bern, North Carolina](/wiki/New_Bern,_North_Carolina "New Bern, North Carolina")
* [Susanna Julie von Bondeli](/wiki/Julie_Bondeli "Julie Bondeli") (1731--1778) -- famous salonist and lady of letters, the salon became the center of intellectual life in Bern.
* [Grand Duchess Anna Feodorovna of Russia](/wiki/Princess_Juliane_of_Saxe-Coburg-Saalfeld "Princess Juliane of Saxe-Coburg-Saalfeld") (1781 -- Elfenau, near Bern 1860) -- German princess of the ducal house of Saxe-Coburg-Saalfeld
* [Mikhail Bakunin](/wiki/Mikhail_Bakunin "Mikhail Bakunin") (1814-- 1876 in Bern) -- Russian revolutionary anarchist.^[\[66\]](#cite_note-72)^{#cite_ref-72}
* [Karl Schenk](/wiki/Karl_Schenk "Karl Schenk") (1823--1895) -- pastor, politician; served on the Swiss Federal Council 1863--1895
* [Vladimir Lenin](/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin "Vladimir Lenin") (1870--1924) -- lived in Bern 1914--1917
* [Louise Elisabeth de Meuron](/wiki/Louise_Elisabeth_de_Meuron "Louise Elisabeth de Meuron") (1882--1980) -- aristocrat and eccentric personality in Bern
* Dom [Duarte Pio, Duke of Braganza](/wiki/Duarte_Pio,_Duke_of_Braganza "Duarte Pio, Duke of Braganza") (born 1945) -- claimant to the defunct Portuguese throne, as the head of the [House of Braganza](/wiki/House_of_Braganza "House of Braganza")
* [Regula Rytz](/wiki/Regula_Rytz "Regula Rytz") (born 1962) -- politician, sociologist and historian^[\[67\]](#cite_note-woz-20111110-73)^{#cite_ref-woz-20111110_73-0}
* [Ursula Wyss](/wiki/Ursula_Wyss "Ursula Wyss") (born 1973) -- economist and politician
* [Min Li Marti](/wiki/Min_Li_Marti "Min Li Marti") (born 1974) -- politician, publisher, sociologist and historian

### Science and academia {#Science_and_academia}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=40 "Edit section: Science and academia")\]

* [Albrecht von Haller](/wiki/Albrecht_von_Haller "Albrecht von Haller") (1708--1777) -- anatomist, physiologist, naturalist, bibliographer and poet^[\[68\]](#cite_note-74)^{#cite_ref-74}
* [Carl Adolf Otth](/wiki/Carl_Adolf_Otth "Carl Adolf Otth") (1803--1839) -- [naturalist](/wiki/Naturalist "Naturalist")
* [Gustav Heinrich Otth](/wiki/Gustav_Heinrich_Otth "Gustav Heinrich Otth") (1806--1874) -- [mycologist](/wiki/Mycologist "Mycologist")
* [Carl Brunner von Wattenwyl](/wiki/Carl_Brunner_von_Wattenwyl "Carl Brunner von Wattenwyl") (1823--1914) -- entomologist who specialised in [Orthoptera](/wiki/Orthoptera "Orthoptera")
* [Ludwig Fischer](/wiki/Ludwig_Fischer_(botanist) "Ludwig Fischer (botanist)") (1828--1907) -- botanist, researched [phanerogams](/wiki/Phanerogams "Phanerogams") and [cryptogams](/wiki/Cryptogams "Cryptogams")
* [Adolph Francis Alphonse Bandelier](/wiki/Adolph_Francis_Alphonse_Bandelier "Adolph Francis Alphonse Bandelier") (1840--1914) -- American archaeologist.^[\[69\]](#cite_note-75)^{#cite_ref-75}
* [Emil Theodor Kocher](/wiki/Emil_Theodor_Kocher "Emil Theodor Kocher") (1841--1917) -- physician and medical researcher, received the 1909 [Nobel Prize in Physiology or Medicine](/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Physiology_or_Medicine "Nobel Prize in Physiology or Medicine") for work on the thyroid^[\[70\]](#cite_note-76)^{#cite_ref-76}
* [Arnold Klebs](/wiki/Arnold_Klebs "Arnold Klebs") (1870--1943) -- physician who specialized in the study of [tuberculosis](/wiki/Tuberculosis "Tuberculosis")
* [Anna Tumarkin](/wiki/Anna_Tumarkin "Anna Tumarkin") (1875--1951) -- Russian-born, naturalized Swiss academic, the first woman to become a professor of philosophy at the [University of Bern](/wiki/University_of_Bern "University of Bern")
* [Albert Einstein](/wiki/Albert_Einstein "Albert Einstein") (1879--1955) -- worked out his [theory of relativity](/wiki/Theory_of_relativity "Theory of relativity") while living in Bern, employed as a [patent examiner](/wiki/Patent_examiner "Patent examiner") at the [patent office](/wiki/Swiss_Federal_Institute_of_Intellectual_Property "Swiss Federal Institute of Intellectual Property")
* [Ida Hoff](/wiki/Ida_Hoff "Ida Hoff") (1880--1952) -- pioneering doctor, a feminist activist, an early regular female motorist
* [Aimé Félix Tschiffely](/wiki/Aim%C3%A9_F%C3%A9lix_Tschiffely "Aimé Félix Tschiffely") (1895--1954) -- Swiss-born, Argentine professor, writer and equestrian adventurer
* [Hans Albert Einstein](/wiki/Hans_Albert_Einstein "Hans Albert Einstein") (1904--1973) -- Swiss-American engineer and educator, the second child and first son of [Albert Einstein](/wiki/Albert_Einstein "Albert Einstein")
* [Friedrich Tinner](/wiki/Friedrich_Tinner "Friedrich Tinner") (born 1937) -- nuclear engineer connected with the proliferation of nuclear materials in Iran, Libya, and North Korea
* [Claudia Rosiny](/wiki/Claudia_Rosiny "Claudia Rosiny") (born 1960) -- German-Swiss academic in Dance and Media studies, a festival director and cultural manager
* [Daniel Mojon](/wiki/Daniel_Mojon "Daniel Mojon") (born 1963) -- ophthalmologist and ophthalmic surgeon, invented minimally-invasive [strabismus surgery](/wiki/Strabismus_surgery "Strabismus surgery")
* [Peter Jüni](/wiki/Peter_J%C3%BCni "Peter Jüni") (born  1975) - scientific director of the Ontario COVID-19 Science Advisory Table, works at [St. Michael's Hospital (Toronto)](/wiki/St._Michael%27s_Hospital_(Toronto) "St. Michael's Hospital (Toronto)")

### Writing and acting {#Writing_and_acting}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=41 "Edit section: Writing and acting")\]

* [Ulrich Boner](/wiki/Ulrich_Boner "Ulrich Boner") or Bonerius (early 14th century) -- German-speaking Swiss writer of fable^[\[71\]](#cite_note-77)^{#cite_ref-77}
* [Hans von Rüte](/wiki/Hans_von_R%C3%BCte "Hans von Rüte") (died 1558) -- Bernese dramatist and chronicler of the Swiss Reformation
* [Johann David Wyss](/wiki/Johann_David_Wyss "Johann David Wyss") (1743--1818) -- author, best remembered for [The Swiss Family Robinson](/wiki/The_Swiss_Family_Robinson "The Swiss Family Robinson")
* [Charles Victor de Bonstetten](/wiki/Charles_Victor_de_Bonstetten "Charles Victor de Bonstetten") (1745--1832) -- liberal writer^[\[72\]](#cite_note-78)^{#cite_ref-78}
* [Daniel Albert Wyttenbach](/wiki/Daniel_Albert_Wyttenbach "Daniel Albert Wyttenbach") (1746--1820) -- German Swiss classical scholar^[\[73\]](#cite_note-79)^{#cite_ref-79}
* [Johann Rudolf Wyss](/wiki/Johann_Rudolf_Wyss "Johann Rudolf Wyss") (1782--1830) -- author, writer, and folklorist who wrote the words to the former Swiss national anthem^[\[74\]](#cite_note-80)^{#cite_ref-80}
* [Charles Monnard](/wiki/Charles_Monnard "Charles Monnard") (1790--1865) -- historian and member of the [Helvetic Society](/wiki/Helvetic_Society "Helvetic Society")
* [Vincent O. Carter](/wiki/Vincent_O._Carter "Vincent O. Carter") (1924--1983) -- American writer, author of *The Bern Book* ^[\[75\]](#cite_note-81)^{#cite_ref-81}
* [Selma Urfer](/wiki/Selma_Urfer "Selma Urfer") (1928--2013) -- author, translator and actress^[\[76\]](#cite_note-82)^{#cite_ref-82}
* [Liselotte Pulver](/wiki/Liselotte_Pulver "Liselotte Pulver") (born 1929) -- actress, well known for her hearty and joyful laughter^[\[77\]](#cite_note-83)^{#cite_ref-83}
* [Bigna Francis-von Wyttenbach](/w/index.php?title=Bigna_Francis-von_Wyttenbach&action=edit&redlink=1 "Bigna Francis-von Wyttenbach (page does not exist)") (1930--2021) -- Swiss writer
* [Yves Rénier](/wiki/Yves_R%C3%A9nier "Yves Rénier") (1942--2021) -- French actor, director, screenwriter and voice actor^[\[78\]](#cite_note-84)^{#cite_ref-84}
* [Lukas Hartmann](/wiki/Lukas_Hartmann "Lukas Hartmann") (born 1944) -- children's writer, Switzerland's "first husband" in 2015
* [Yang Lian](/wiki/Yang_Lian_(poet) "Yang Lian (poet)") (born 1955) -- Swiss-Chinese poet associated with the [Misty Poets](/wiki/Misty_Poets "Misty Poets")
* [Sibylle Canonica](/wiki/Sibylle_Canonica "Sibylle Canonica") (born 1957) -- actress, has appeared in more than forty films since 1981^[\[79\]](#cite_note-85)^{#cite_ref-85}
* [Georges Delnon](/wiki/Georges_Delnon "Georges Delnon") (born 1958) -- theatre director, artistic director and professor
* [Sabine Timoteo](/wiki/Sabine_Timoteo "Sabine Timoteo") (born 1975) -- actress^[\[80\]](#cite_note-86)^{#cite_ref-86}
* [Yangzom Brauen](/wiki/Yangzom_Brauen "Yangzom Brauen") (born 1980) -- actress, activist and writer^[\[81\]](#cite_note-87)^{#cite_ref-87}
* [Cleo von Adelsheim](/wiki/Cleo_von_Adelsheim "Cleo von Adelsheim") (born 1987) -- German-Chilean actress^[\[82\]](#cite_note-88)^{#cite_ref-88}

### Artists, painters and musicians {#Artists.2C_painters_and_musicians}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=42 "Edit section: Artists, painters and musicians")\]

* [Niklaus Manuel Deutsch](/wiki/Niklaus_Manuel_Deutsch "Niklaus Manuel Deutsch") ( 1484--1530) -- artist, writer, mercenary and Reformed politician
* [Albrecht Kauw](/wiki/Albrecht_Kauw "Albrecht Kauw") (1621--1681) -- still-life painter, cartographer and a painter of [vedute](/wiki/Vedute "Vedute")
* [Gabriel Lory](/wiki/Gabriel_Lory "Gabriel Lory") the Elder (1763--1840) -- Bernese landscape painter and illustrator
* [Ferdinand Hodler](/wiki/Ferdinand_Hodler "Ferdinand Hodler") (1853--1918) -- painter of portraits, landscapes and genre paintings
* [Lisa Wenger](/wiki/Lisa_Wenger "Lisa Wenger") (1858--1941) -- painter and author of children's books
* [Adolf Wölfli](/wiki/Adolf_W%C3%B6lfli "Adolf Wölfli") (1864--1930) -- artist associated with [Art brut](/wiki/Art_brut "Art brut")
* [Bertha Zuricher](/wiki/Bertha_Zuricher "Bertha Zuricher") (1869--1949) -- author, painter and engraver
* [Volkmar Andreae](/wiki/Volkmar_Andreae "Volkmar Andreae") (1879--1962) -- conductor and composer
* [Eric Blom](/wiki/Eric_Blom "Eric Blom") CBE (1888--1959) -- British-naturalised music lexicographer, musicologist, music critic and music [biographer](/wiki/The_New_Grove_Dictionary_of_Music_and_Musicians "The New Grove Dictionary of Music and Musicians")
* [Klaus Huber](/wiki/Klaus_Huber "Klaus Huber") (1924--2017) -- composer and academic
* [Margrit Zimmermann](/wiki/Margrit_Zimmermann "Margrit Zimmermann") (1927--2020) -- pianist, composer, conductor and music educator
* [Mani Matter](/wiki/Mani_Matter "Mani Matter") (1936--1972) -- singer-songwriter^[\[83\]](#cite_note-89)^{#cite_ref-89}
* [Roland Zoss](/wiki/Roland_Zoss "Roland Zoss") (born 1951) -- songwriter and novelist, lives on the [Aeolian Islands](/wiki/Aeolian_Islands "Aeolian Islands")
* [Christine Lauterburg](/wiki/Christine_Lauterburg "Christine Lauterburg") (born 1956) -- singer, yodeler and actress^[\[84\]](#cite_note-90)^{#cite_ref-90}
* [Patricia Kopatchinskaja](/wiki/Patricia_Kopatchinskaja "Patricia Kopatchinskaja") (born 1977) -- Moldovan-Austrian-Swiss violinist
* [Zora Slokar](https://de.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zora_Slokar "de:Zora Slokar"), (born 1980) horn player with [Orchestra della Svizzera Italiana](/wiki/Orchestra_della_Svizzera_Italiana "Orchestra della Svizzera Italiana")
* [Luca Hänni](/wiki/Luca_H%C3%A4nni "Luca Hänni") (born 1994) -- singer-songwriter, dancer, and model, Swiss representative at the [2019 Eurovision Song Contest](/wiki/Eurovision_Song_Contest_2019 "Eurovision Song Contest 2019")
* [Giuseppe Bausilio](/wiki/Giuseppe_Bausilio "Giuseppe Bausilio") (born 1997) -- actor, dancer, and singer^[\[85\]](#cite_note-91)^{#cite_ref-91}

### Business {#Business}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=43 "Edit section: Business")\]

* [Johann Rudolf Tschiffeli](/wiki/Johann_Rudolf_Tschiffeli "Johann Rudolf Tschiffeli") (1716--1780) -- agronomist, a wealthy merchant, economist, and lawyer
* [Franz Rudolf Frisching](/wiki/Franz_Rudolf_Frisching "Franz Rudolf Frisching") (1733--1807) -- Bernese patrician, officer, politician, founded the [Frisching Faience Manufactory](/wiki/Frisching_Faience_Manufactory "Frisching Faience Manufactory")
* [Rodolphe Lindt](/wiki/Rodolphe_Lindt "Rodolphe Lindt") (1855--1909) -- chocolate manufacturer, founded the [Lindt chocolate factory](/wiki/Lindt_%26_Spr%C3%BCngli "Lindt & Sprüngli")
* [Marianne Alvoni](/wiki/Marianne_Alvoni "Marianne Alvoni") (born 1964) -- fashion designer

### Sport {#Sport}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=44 "Edit section: Sport")\]
[![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Otto_Hess_by_Carl_Horner.jpg/140px-Otto_Hess_by_Carl_Horner.jpg)](/wiki/File:Otto_Hess_by_Carl_Horner.jpg) Otto Hess, c. 1906 [![](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Jenni_2013-04-15.JPG/140px-Jenni_2013-04-15.JPG)](/wiki/File:Jenni_2013-04-15.JPG) Jennifer Oehrli, 2013

* [Elia Alessandrini](/wiki/Elia_Alessandrini "Elia Alessandrini") (1997--2022), footballer, prospect player for the [Switzerland national football team](/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team "Switzerland national football team"), died from drowning in Oman
* [Philippe Marie Eugène, Count d'Ursel](/wiki/Philippe_d%27Ursel "Philippe d'Ursel") (1920--2017), was a Swiss-born Belgian alpine skier and a member of the [Ursel family](/wiki/Ursel_family "Ursel family"), competed at the [1948 Winter Olympics](/wiki/1948_Winter_Olympics "1948 Winter Olympics")
* [Tanja Frieden](/wiki/Tanja_Frieden "Tanja Frieden") (born 1976), snowboarder and gold medallist at the [2006 Winter Olympics](/wiki/2006_Winter_Olympics "2006 Winter Olympics")
* [Guerino Gottardi](/wiki/Guerino_Gottardi "Guerino Gottardi") (born 1970), a retired Swiss-Italian footballer, almost 250 club caps
* [Otto Hess](/wiki/Otto_Hess "Otto Hess") (1878--1926), pitcher for the [Cleveland Bronchos](/wiki/Cleveland_Bronchos "Cleveland Bronchos") 1902 and 1904--08 and [Boston Braves](/wiki/History_of_the_Boston_Braves "History of the Boston Braves") 1912--15
* [Maurizio Jacobacci](/wiki/Maurizio_Jacobacci "Maurizio Jacobacci") (born 1963), Italian-Swiss football manager and former player
* [Roman Josi](/wiki/Roman_Josi "Roman Josi") (born 1990), professional ice hockey player, selected to play for Switzerland at the [2010 Winter Olympics](/wiki/2010_Winter_Olympics "2010 Winter Olympics")
* [Arnold Käch](/wiki/Arnold_K%C3%A4ch "Arnold Käch") (1914--1998), military officer, skier, ski official and writer
* [Christian Kauter](/wiki/Christian_Kauter "Christian Kauter") (born 1947), fencer, silver medallist in the team épée at the [1972 Summer Olympics](/wiki/1972_Summer_Olympics "1972 Summer Olympics") and bronze medallist at the [1976 Summer Olympics](/wiki/1976_Summer_Olympics "1976 Summer Olympics")
* [Dominik Märki](/wiki/Dominik_M%C3%A4rki "Dominik Märki") (born 1990), Swiss curler, living in [Fayetteville, Arkansas](/wiki/Fayetteville,_Arkansas "Fayetteville, Arkansas"), bronze medallist in the [2018 Winter Olympics](/wiki/2018_Winter_Olympics "2018 Winter Olympics")
* [Jürg Marmet](/wiki/J%C3%BCrg_Marmet "Jürg Marmet") (1927--2013), mountaineer, part of the first two-man Swiss team which climbed [Mount Everest](/wiki/Mount_Everest "Mount Everest") in 1956
* [Benoît Musy](/wiki/Beno%C3%AEt_Musy "Benoît Musy") (1917--1956), racing driver and motorcycle racer
* [Maja Neuenschwander](/wiki/Maja_Neuenschwander "Maja Neuenschwander") (born 1980), long-distance runner who competes in marathon races
* [Jennifer Oehrli](/wiki/Jennifer_Oehrli "Jennifer Oehrli") (born 1989), football goalkeeper, member of the [Switzerland women's national football team](/wiki/Switzerland_women%27s_national_football_team "Switzerland women's national football team")
* [Mirjam Ott](/wiki/Mirjam_Ott "Mirjam Ott") (born 1972), retired curler, captain of the Swiss Olympic Curling Team
* [Kris Richard](/wiki/Kris_Richard_(racing_driver) "Kris Richard (racing driver)") (born 1994), racing driver
* [Markus Ryffel](/wiki/Markus_Ryffel "Markus Ryffel") (born 1955), former long-distance runner, silver medallist in the 5000 metres at the [1984 Summer Olympics](/wiki/1984_Summer_Olympics "1984 Summer Olympics")
* [Akira Schmid](/wiki/Akira_Schmid "Akira Schmid") (born 2000), professional ice hockey goaltender with the [New Jersey Devils](/wiki/New_Jersey_Devils "New Jersey Devils") of the [National Hockey League](/wiki/National_Hockey_League "National Hockey League")
* [Ernst Schmied](/wiki/Ernst_Schmied "Ernst Schmied") (1924--2002), mountaineer, the second successful summiteer of [Mount Everest](/wiki/Mount_Everest "Mount Everest") in 1956
* [Esther Staubli](/wiki/Esther_Staubli "Esther Staubli") (born 1979), football referee, on the FIFA International Referees List since 2006
* [Willi Steffen](/wiki/Willi_Steffen "Willi Steffen") (1925--2005), former fighter pilot and international footballer, won 28 caps for his country
* [Christine Stückelberger](/wiki/Christine_St%C3%BCckelberger "Christine Stückelberger") (born 1947), retired equestrian, gold medallist in dressage at the [1976 Summer Olympics](/wiki/1976_Summer_Olympics "1976 Summer Olympics") compete at six Olympics: 1972, 1976, 1984, 1988, 1996 and 2000.
* [Alain Sutter](/wiki/Alain_Sutter "Alain Sutter") (born 1968), footballer, 351 club caps, 58 national team caps

Notes and references {#Notes_and_references}
--------------------------------------------

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=46 "Edit section: Notes and references")\]  

### Notes {#Notes}

\[[edit](/w/index.php?title=Bern&action=edit&section=47 "Edit section: Notes")\]  
1. **[\^](#cite_ref-3)** [Alemannic German](/wiki/Alemannic_German_language "Alemannic German language"): *Bärn* [\[b̥æːrn\]](/wiki/Help:IPA/Alemannic_German "Help:IPA/Alemannic German"); [Arpitan](/wiki/Arpitan_language "Arpitan language"): *Bèrna* [\[ˈbɛʁna\]](/wiki/Help:IPA/Franco-Proven%C3%A7al "Help:IPA/Franco-Provençal") [](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/c/c1/Frp-greverin-B%C3%AArna.ogg/Frp-greverin-B%C3%AArna.ogg.mp3 "Play audio")^[ⓘ](/wiki/File:Frp-greverin-B%C3%AArna.ogg "File:Frp-greverin-Bêrna.ogg")^; [Italian](/wiki/Italian_language "Italian language"): *Berna* [\[ˈbɛrna\]](/wiki/Help:IPA/Italian "Help:IPA/Italian"); [Romansh](/wiki/Romansh_language "Romansh language"): *Berna* [\[ˈbɛrnɐ\]](/wiki/Help:IPA/Romansh "Help:IPA/Romansh") [](//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/3/38/Roh-Berna.ogg/Roh-Berna.ogg.mp3 "Play audio")^[ⓘ](/wiki/File:Roh-Berna.ogg "File:Roh-Berna.ogg")^.{#ooui-php-4}
{#cite_note-3}
2. **[\^](#cite_ref-DeFacto_4-0)** Switzerland has no *[de jure](/wiki/De_jure "De jure")* capital{#cite_note-DeFacto-4}
{#cite_note-DeFacto-4}
3. **[\^](#cite_ref-5)** German: *Bundesstadt* ; French: *ville fédérale* ; Italian: *città federale* ; Romansh: *citad federala* . According to the Swiss constitution, the Swiss Confederation intentionally has no "capital", but Bern has governmental institutions such as the [Federal Assembly](/wiki/Federal_Assembly_(Switzerland) "Federal Assembly (Switzerland)") and [Federal Council](/wiki/Federal_Council_(Switzerland) "Federal Council (Switzerland)"). However, the [Federal Supreme Court](/wiki/Federal_Supreme_Court_of_Switzerland "Federal Supreme Court of Switzerland") is in [Lausanne](/wiki/Lausanne "Lausanne"), the [Federal Criminal Court](/wiki/Federal_Criminal_Court_of_Switzerland "Federal Criminal Court of Switzerland") is in [Bellinzona](/wiki/Bellinzona "Bellinzona") and the [Federal Administrative Court](/wiki/Federal_Administrative_Court_(Switzerland) "Federal Administrative Court (Switzerland)") and the [Federal Patent Court](/wiki/Federal_Patent_Court_(Switzerland) "Federal Patent Court (Switzerland)") are in [St. Gallen](/wiki/St._Gallen "St. Gallen"), exemplifying the federal nature of the Confederation.{#cite_note-5}
{#cite_note-5}
4. **[\^](#cite_ref-10)** The official language in any municipality in German-speaking Switzerland is always German. In this context, the term 'German' is used as an umbrella term for any variety of German. So, according to law, people are allowed to communicate with the authorities by using any kind of German, in written or oral form. However, the authorities will always use [Swiss Standard German](/wiki/Swiss_Standard_German "Swiss Standard German") (aka the Swiss variety of [Standard German](/wiki/Standard_German "Standard German")) in documents, or any written form. And orally, it is either *Hochdeutsch* (i.e., Swiss Standard German or what the particular speaker considers as *High German*), or then it depends on the speaker's origin, which dialectal variant they are using.{#cite_note-10}
{#cite_note-10}
